 unke lekhan se jeenyu or hyderabad central uniwarsity jaise campus main desh kii vighatnkaaree takaton, nijee azaadi ke naam par manamaane vyavhaar, nijee azaadi ke naam par aatankiyon ko chhodane, bharat ke abhinn ang jammu-kashmir kii azaadi kii baat karne vaale ko majbooti milti he
 Dr
 guha kii kitabon se kuch vivaditon ansh bhi yahaan die ja rahe hai

 Ramchandra Guha has been appointed as Director by Winter School of Ahmedabad University, the University which has always kept the interest of students at the center, Dr
 ramchandra guha ko niyukt kiya ja rahaa he, guha chaatro ko maanavtaa kii koun si shiksha denge yah gambhir prashn he
 The Akhil Bharatiya Vidyarthi Parishad believes that under the direction of such a directionless person, the youth power of the country will not have any feelings towards the country, will not believe in our culture
 agar aisa vyakti aapke santhaan kii madad se deshvirohi gatividhiyon or bharat ko todane kii gatividhiyon ke saath sahyog kare, tab vidhyaarthee parishad aapke santhaan ke khilaaf bada andolan karegi or iske liye sirf aap zimmedaar honge
 The Akhil Bharatiya Vidyarthi Parishad insists that you ramchandra guha kii niyukti ko tatkaal prabhaav se radd kar den
 Praveen Desai, Metropolitan Minister akhil bhartiya vidhyaarthee parishad The letter has also been sent to the Governor of Gujarat, Chief Minister, Education Minister, Principal Secretary, Department of Education, Board of Governors of Ahmedabad University, Sanjay Lalbhai, Sudhir Mehta, Anjuben Sharma and Pankaj Patel
 patr main jis tarah se dow ramchandra guha ko bharat virdohi, hindu samskruti virdohi bataaya gaya he, ganimat he ki akhil bhartiya vidhyaarthee parishad ne pradhanmantri or raashtrapati se unhen desh se nikaal dene kii maang nahin kii he
 This is a good thing in this
 lekin aap sochie ki raajnneetik taur par abivipi ko kisi se bhi etraz yaa asahmati rakhane kaa puraa haq he, magar vah is aadhaar par kisi kii niyukti roak de to behatar he ki aap vahi padhein jo abivipi kahe
 Rather, get your syllabus also made by ABVP
 kya aapako pataa he ki dilli vishvavidhyalay kii academik maamalon kii standing cameti ne eme polytical science ke chaatro ke liye jo kitaaben padhai jaati hai usamen se dalit shabd hataane ke aadesh die hai
 Instead of Dalit, Bahujan, Ambedkarite or Scheduled Caste will be used
 yahi nahin kaancha ilaiya shefrd kii kitaab ko bhi polytical science ke course se hataa diya gaya he
 Manisha Tiwari has written in the wire that in the meeting of the Standing Committee, a proposal was passed that Ilaiah's books be removed because they allegedly dishonor Hinduism
 isi news website par dilli vishvavidlaay ke polytical science vibhaag main padhaane vaale en sukumaar ne apana paksh rakhaa he
 His side is that till the time, only Manu, Kautilya, Tagore, Gandhi Savarkar have been taught in the Department of Political Science
 lekin maine ek nayaa course banaaya jiskaa naam tha dalit bahujan polytical thot
 In which Gautam Buddha, Jyotiba Phule, Ambedkar, Periyar, Tarabhai Shinde, Kanshi Ram are taught
 isamen anya vidwaanon ke saath kaancha ilaiya kii bhi kitaab he
 The ruling establishment is troubled by questions raised by Dalit scholars
 hoicourt ke aadesh ke baad dalit shabd kaa istamaal nahin ho saktaa he
 Therefore, the word Dalit is being removed
 lekin kaancha ilaiya kii kitaab kya isliye hataane kaa faisla hua he kyonki hindu dharm kaa apmaan karti hai
 Dr
 ramchandra guha par bhi par isi tarah ke aarope hai
 Look through the books of Kancha Ilaiah, you will get a deep and new view of understanding the society
 ab aate hai rafaal vimaan vivaad par
 a new report has come out in The Wire of Rohini Singh and Ravi Nair, which has deepened the questions about the Rafale dispute
 rohinee singh or ravi nair ne ek baat pakadi jo abhi tak saamne nahin ai thi
 Both have written that the Rafale aircraft maker has made a profit of Rs 284 crore by purchasing 35% stake in RDL, another defunct company of Anil Ambani
 is company kaa ladaaku vimaan banane se koi lenaa dena nahin he
 Reliance Defense had an agreement with Dasso Avishen, but why did Dasso buy the shares of a defunct company
 di vir kii report ke anusaar jis company main dasso ne nivesh kiya he wo ghate main chal rahi he or uskaa rajasav shunya he
 Not only this, the public filing by Reliance Infra shows that it has made 34 of RDL in FY 2017-18
 7 pratishat share beche hai
 You can read the full report on The Wire
 is report ke baad rahul gandhi khud press conference karne aae or sarkaar par nae sandarbhon main aarope lagaae
 The comments rahul ne kaha, 'rafel ke siio ne kaha tha kii echel ko pare karke anil ambani ko contract dene kaa kaaran tha ki anil ambani ke paas jameen thi
 Now it is known that ten people poured in Anil Ambani's company for 284 crores and with the same money, Anil Ambani bought the land means that the default is clearly lying
 bada sawaal uthta he ki 8 lakh kii company main jo kuch nahin kar rahi los mekking company he usamen 284 karod rupye dasolt ne kyon daale
 This is called kickback
 so, dis ij da first kickbac givan tu mistar ambani by dasolt
 and it is clear like day

 jangal kii aag se niklaa dhuaan ban rahaa karantasviren or video soshal media par virlaindonesia kaa aasmaan laal hota ja rahaa he
 It looks like red Mars
 log laal rang main duube hue shaharon, sadakon or gaanvon kii tasviren soshal media par viral kar rahe hai
 But this red color is a sign of danger
 logon ke ankhon or gale main jalan or dard kii shikaayat bad gai he
 Because this red color is formed due to the smoke sheet spread by the forest fire
 is chadar kii chapet main dakshin purv asia kaa bada ilaaka aa jaataa he
 There has been a continuous fire in Indonesia for the past 8 months
 isse 328,724 hectare jameen-jangal khaak ho chuke hai
 This is why so much smoke is spread
 aaie jaanate hai ki aakhir aasmaan aise laal rang main kyon badal gaya
 
 
 In meteorological language, it is called Rayleigh scattering
 yani prakaash kii kirnon ke bikharane kii vajah se aisa hota he
 The color of the sky changes when the particles present in the smoke change their color when light comes on
 dhuen main maujuud adhiktar kan aakaar main kareeb 1 micrometer ke hote hai
 Some are even smaller particles
 inkaa aakaar 0
 05 micrometers in size or less, which is high in smoke
 yahi akaash main suraj kii roshni padate hi laal rang main badal jate hai
 So you start seeing red color instead of blue in the sky
 jo tasviren viral hui hai ve dopaher main lee gai thim
 Therefore, red color is more visible
 lekin vahaan taapmaana baraabar hi tha
